##############################################
###### Monarchy Reform Tier 2
##############################################	

country_event = {

	id = iv_reform_events.1
	title = iv_reform_events.1a
	desc = iv_reform_events.1b
	
	picture = BIG_BOOK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1c"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_wirt
		}
		
	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1d"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_rat
		}

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1e"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_politik1
		}

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1f"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_stateorga
		}	

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1g"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_inner
		}	

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1h"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_aussen
		}	

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1i"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_expan
		}	

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1j"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_handel
		}	

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1k"
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_tier_2_estate
		}	

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.1z" # brauchte mehr Zeit (deswegen letzte Option)

		}		
		
}

					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_rep_tier_9_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_rep_tier_10_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_rep_tier_11_grundrechte

					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_rep_tier_13_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_rep_tier_14_grundrechte
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_rep_tier_10_vision
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_rep_tier_11_vision
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_rep_tier_12_vision

					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_7_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_8_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_9_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_10_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_11_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_12_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_13_grundrechte
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_14_grundrechte
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_10_vision
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_11_vision
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_12_vision
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_13_vision
					has_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_14_vision
					}
				}		
		}
			set_country_flag = iv_gov_reform_theo_tier_15_vision
		}		

	option = {
		name = "iv_reform_events.40z" # brauchte mehr Zeit (deswegen letzte Option)

		}
